<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Oberon, or The Elf-King's Oath
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Romantic and Fairy Opera in 3 Acts
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Weber,_Carl_Maria_von" title="Category:Weber, Carl Maria von">Weber, Carl Maria von</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>J.306
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>ICW 49
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 acts
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1825-26
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1826-04-12 in London, Covent Garden
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1826 (vocal score); 1874 (full score)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Planch%C3%A9,_James_Robinson" title="Category:Planché, James Robinson">James Robinson Planché</a> (1796–1880)
<dl><dd>after <a href="/wiki/Category:Wieland,_Christoph_Martin" title="Category:Wieland, Christoph Martin">Christoph Martin Wieland</a> (1733–1813)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>English
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>voices, mixed chorus, orchestra <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dd><i>Cast</i>
<dl><dd>Oberon (tenor)<br />Titania (actress)<br />Puck (mezzo-soprano)<br />Sir John of Bordeaux (tenor)<br />Sherasmin (baritone)<br />Rezia (soprano)<br />Fatima (mezzo-soprano)<br />Two Mermaids (mezzo-soprano)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Mixed Chorus</i> 
<dl><dd>Faries, ladies, knights, guards, slaves, mermaids etc.
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Orchestra</i> </div>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
